()tsa() myu gu chos can /

mu dang po 'gog pa ni /
mig dbang gis mig dbang gnyis pa kho na skyed dam mig shes gcig bu kho na skyed /

mu gnyis pa 'gog pa ni /
mig shes kyi myong ba'i cha ni de ma thag rkyen gyi lag rjes dang /
yul gyi rnam pa shar ba'i cha ni dmigs rkyen gyi lag rjes dang /
yul ris su chad pa 'dzin nus pa'i cha ni bdag rkyen kyi lag rjes ma yin par thal /
don dam par rgyu gcig kho nas 'bras bu du ma skyed pa'i phyir /
mu gsum pa 'gog pa ni /
rgyu du mas 'bras bu gcig kho na skyed na mig shes kyi myong ba'i cha dang yul gyi rnam pa shar ba'i cha dang yul ris su chad pa 'dzin nus kyi cha gsum po'i nang nas gang rung gcig kho na mig shes kyi rkyen gsum ka'i lag rjes su thal bas /

()tsha() 'dir 'phags pa kun dga' bo'i rgyud kyi bdag dang dge slong dang mi dang rgyun zhugs dang sh+'+k+ya ba rnams don gcig ma yin pa rab shad pa ltar dbu ma'i mtha' dpyod las kyang da lta'i rgyal po slar bcas ldan dge slong byas pa gcig gi rgyud kyi tshe 'di'i bdag dang mi dang rgyal po dang dge slong rnams yin khyab mnyam ma yin par bshad pa ni sgra ji bzhin par khas len mi rung ste /

la la na re /

stong nyid rgyu 'bras bu 'gro tshul shes dgos la /

don dam par @# / /
rgyu gcig gis 'bras bu gcig bskyed pa min zhing /

rten 'byung min pa'i chos ni lugs 'dir med la /
rten 'byung ni phrad nas grub pa dang ltos nas grub pa dang brten nas grub pa tsam yin pa'i phyir gzugs sogs phyi nang gi chos kun tshugs thub dang rang ngos nas grub pa rnams min no zhes pa ni /
bsgrub bya'i chos kyi don yid la byed pa der zab po'i nyams len dang gtan tshig kyi don yid la byed pa der rgya che ba'i nyams len tshang zhing /
rim bzhin rtag pa dang chad pa'i mtha' gnyis sel ba'i phyir 'di ni rigs pa'i rgyal po yin no / /

sgra bshad ni /
